.. _ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t029c009_f:

Average weeks worked in 2010 (female)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------











Measure "Average weeks worked in 2010 (female)"  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t029c009_f'
      );






Average weeks worked in 2010 (female) is only available for point lookups.

.. _ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t004c001_f:

Total labour force aged 15 years and over (female)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------





Refers to whether an employed person is an employee or is self-employed. The self-employed include persons with or without a business, as well as unpaid family workers.





Measure "Total labour force aged 15 years and over (female)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t004c001_f'
      );





Measure "Total labour force aged 15 years and over (female)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
          'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t004c001_f'
        );

^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(

          'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t004c003_f'
        );






Measure "Labour force aged 15+ - All classes of worker (female)" percent of "Total labour force aged 15 years and over (female)" at one point:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t004c003_f',
        'denominator'
      );

      OBS_GetMeasure(
        ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),

        'denominator'

""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""""





This category includes employed persons who usually worked less than 30 hours per week, at their main or only job.





Measure "Worked part-time in 2010 (female)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t007c005_f'
      );





Measure "Worked part-time in 2010 (female)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
          'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t007c005_f'
        );

  UPDATE {table_name}

        'denominator'
      );

.. _ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t004c001_m:

Total labour force aged 15 years and over (male)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------





Refers to whether an employed person is an employee or is self-employed. The self-employed include persons with or without a business, as well as unpaid family workers.





Measure "Total labour force aged 15 years and over (male)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t004c001_m'
      );





Measure "Total labour force aged 15 years and over (male)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
          'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t004c001_m'
        );

.. _ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t004c001_t:

Total labour force aged 15 years and over (total)
------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------





Refers to whether an employed person is an employee or is self-employed. The self-employed include persons with or without a business, as well as unpaid family workers.





Measure "Total labour force aged 15 years and over (total)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t004c001_t'
      );





Measure "Total labour force aged 15 years and over (total)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
          'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t004c001_t'
        );

^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^











Measure "Employed (total)"  density per sq. kilometer  for one point:


.. code-block:: postgresql





  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t015c003_t'
      );





Measure "Employed (total)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql

    UPDATE {table_name}
      SET {new_numeric_column} =
        OBS_GetMeasure(
          ST_Buffer(CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307), 0.01),
          'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t015c003_t'
        );






Measure "Employed (total)" percent of "Total population aged 15+ - In the labour force (total)" at one point:

.. code-block:: postgresql

  UPDATE {table_name}
    SET {new_numeric_column} =
      OBS_GetMeasure(
        CDB_LatLng(43.6559499126, -79.3796539307),
        'ca.statcan.cols_nhs.t015c003_t',
        'denominator'
      );


Measure "Employed (total)" percent of "Total population aged 15+ - In the labour force (total)" within an area:

.. code-block:: postgresql
